I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Node names should be rfc1123 compliant even when falling back on os.Hostname()
**Describe the bug**
It is possible to have hostnames for machines contain uppercase characters; even if you keep the hostname for the node name it will be lower cased for rfc1123. 

This causes service node label updates to fail as the node does not exist with that name in k8s.

While this configuration is legacy it also seems reasonable to accommodate as this is a known case.

**To Reproduce**
Deploy k8s with upper case host names and use kube-vip with labeling on nodes.

**Expected behavior**
When looking for a node it should give best effort and not intentionally just use a bad value.

**Screenshots**
If applicable, add screenshots to help explain your problem.

**Environment (please complete the following information):**
 - OS/Distro: [e.g. Ubuntu 1804]
 - Kubernetes Version: [e.g. v.1.18]
 - Kube-vip Version: [e.g. 0.2.3]

**`Kube-vip.yaml`:**
If Possible add in your kube-vip manifest (please remove anything that is confidential)

**Additional context**
Add any other context about the problem here.

</pr_description>

    38	
    39	// Manager degines the manager of the load-balancing services
    40	type Manager struct {
    41	        clientSet   *kubernetes.Clientset
    42	        rwClientSet *kubernetes.Clientset
    43	        configMap   string
    44	        config      *kubevip.Config
    45	
    46	        // Manager services
    47	        // service bool
    48	
    49	        // BGP Manager, this is a singleton that manages all BGP advertisements
    50	        bgpServer *bgp.Server
    51	
    52	        // This channel is used to catch an OS signal and trigger a shutdown
    53	        signalChan chan os.Signal
    54	
    55	        sigint sync.Once
    56	
    57	        svcProcessor *services.Processor
    58	
    59	        // This is a prometheus counter used to count the number of events received
    60	        // from the service watcher
    61	        countServiceWatchEvent *prometheus.CounterVec
    62	
    63	        // This is a prometheus gauge indicating the state of the sessions.
    64	        // 1 means "ESTABLISHED", 0 means "NOT ESTABLISHED"
    65	        bgpSessionInfoGauge *prometheus.GaugeVec
    66	
    67	        // This mutex is to protect calls from various goroutines
    68	        mutex sync.Mutex
    69	
    70	        // This tracks used network interfaces and guards them with mutex for concurrent changes.
    71	        intfMgr *networkinterface.Manager
    72	
    73	        // This tracks VIPs and performs ARP/NDP advertisement.
    74	        arpMgr *arp.Manager
    75	
    76	        // This tracks node labels and performs label management
    77	        // implementation will be decided in constructor
    78	        // based on config.EnableNodeLabeling
    79	        nodeLabelManager node.LabelManager
    80	
    81	        // This variable reports if manager is being closed
    82	        closing atomic.Bool
    83	
    84	        // Will be used for leaderelection when required
    85	        electionMgr *election.Manager
    86	
    87	        // Will handle leases
    88	        leaseMgr *lease.Manager
    89	}
    90	
    91	// New will create a new managing object
    92	func New(ctx context.Context, configMap string, config *kubevip.Config) (*Manager, error) {
    93	
    94	        // Instance identity should be the same as k8s node name to ensure better compatibility.
    95	        // By default k8s sets node name to `hostname -s`,
    96	        // so if node name is not provided in the config,
    97	        // we set it to hostname as a fallback.
    98	        // This mimics legacy behavior and should work on old kube-vip installations.
    99	        if config.NodeName == "" {
   100	                log.Warn("Node name is missing from the config, fall back to hostname")
   101	                hostname, err := os.Hostname()
   102	                if err != nil {
   103	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not get hostname: %v", err)
   104	                }
   105	                config.NodeName = hostname
   106	        }
   107	        log.Info("using node name", "name", config.NodeName)
   108	
   109	        adminConfigPath := "/etc/kubernetes/admin.conf"
   110	        homeConfigPath := filepath.Join(os.Getenv("HOME"), ".kube", "config")
   111	
   112	        var clientset *kubernetes.Clientset
   113	        var clientConfig *rest.Config
   114	        var err error
   115	
   116	        switch {
   117	        case config.LeaderElectionType == "etcd":
   118	                // Do nothing, we don't construct a k8s client for etcd leader election
   119	        case utils.FileExists(adminConfigPath):
   120	                if config.KubernetesAddr != "" {
   121	                        log.Info("k8s address", "address", config.KubernetesAddr)
   122	                        clientConfig, err = k8s.NewRestConfig(adminConfigPath, false, config.KubernetesAddr)
   123	                } else if config.EnableControlPlane {
   124	                        // If this is a control plane host it will likely have started as a static pod or won't have the
   125	                        // VIP up before trying to connect to the API server, we set the API endpoint to this machine to
   126	                        // ensure connectivity.
   127	                        if config.DetectControlPlane {
   128	                                clientConfig, err = k8s.FindWorkingKubernetesAddress(adminConfigPath, false)
   129	                        } else {
   130	                                // This will attempt to use kubernetes as the hostname (this should be passed as a host alias) in the pod manifest
   131	                                clientConfig, err = k8s.NewRestConfig(adminConfigPath, false, fmt.Sprintf("kubernetes:%v", config.Port))
   132	                        }
   133	                } else {
   134	                        clientConfig, err = k8s.NewRestConfig(adminConfigPath, false, "")
   135	                }
   136	                if err != nil {
   137	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s REST config from external file: %q: %w", adminConfigPath, err)
   138	                }
   139	                if clientset, err = k8s.NewClientset(clientConfig); err != nil {
   140	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s clientset: %w", err)
   141	                }
   142	                log.Debug("Using external Kubernetes configuration from file", "path", adminConfigPath)
   143	        case utils.FileExists(homeConfigPath):
   144	                clientConfig, err = k8s.NewRestConfig(homeConfigPath, false, "")
   145	                if err != nil {
   146	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s REST config from external file: %q: %w", homeConfigPath, err)
   147	                }
   148	                clientset, err = k8s.NewClientset(clientConfig)
   149	                if err != nil {
   150	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s clientset from external file: %q: %w", homeConfigPath, err)
   151	                }
   152	                log.Debug("Using external Kubernetes configuration from file", "path", adminConfigPath)
   153	        default:
   154	                clientConfig, err = k8s.NewRestConfig("", true, "")
   155	                if err != nil {
   156	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s REST config from incluster file: %q: %w", homeConfigPath, err)
   157	                }
   158	                clientset, err = k8s.NewClientset(clientConfig)
   159	                if err != nil {
   160	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s clientset from incluster config: %w", err)
   161	                }
   162	                log.Debug("Using external Kubernetes configuration from incluster config.")
   163	        }
   164	
   165	        var rwClientSet *kubernetes.Clientset
   166	        // if clientConfig is not nil, then we are not using etcd leader election
   167	        // we need to create non-timeout clientset for RetryWatcher
   168	        if clientConfig != nil {
   169	                rwConfig := *clientConfig
   170	                rwConfig.Timeout = 0
   171	                rwClientSet, err = k8s.NewClientset(&rwConfig)
   172	                if err != nil {
   173	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s clientset for retry watcher: %w", err)
   174	                }
   175	        }
   176	
   177	        // Flip this to something else
   178	        // if config.DetectControlPlane {
   179	        //      log.Info("[k8s client] flipping to internal service account")
   180	        //      _, err = clientset.CoreV1().ServiceAccounts("kube-system").Apply(context.TODO(), kubevip.GenerateSA(), v1.ApplyOptions{FieldManager: "application/apply-patch"})
   181	        //      if err != nil {
   182	        //              return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s clientset from incluster config: %v", err)
   183	        //      }
   184	        //      _, err = clientset.RbacV1().ClusterRoles().Apply(context.TODO(), kubevip.GenerateCR(), v1.ApplyOptions{FieldManager: "application/apply-patch"})
   185	        //      if err != nil {
   186	        //              return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s clientset from incluster config: %v", err)
   187	        //      }
   188	        //      _, err = clientset.RbacV1().ClusterRoleBindings().Apply(context.TODO(), kubevip.GenerateCRB(), v1.ApplyOptions{FieldManager: "application/apply-patch"})
   189	        //      if err != nil {
   190	        //              return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s clientset from incluster config: %v", err)
   191	        //      }
   192	        // }
   193	
   194	        // listen for interrupts or the Linux SIGTERM signal and cancel
   195	        // our context, which the leader election code will observe and
   196	        // step down
   197	        signalChan := make(chan os.Signal, 1)
   198	        // Add Notification for Userland interrupt
   199	        signal.Notify(signalChan, syscall.SIGINT)
   200	
   201	        // Add Notification for SIGTERM (sent from Kubernetes)
   202	        signal.Notify(signalChan, syscall.SIGTERM)
   203	
   204	        // Add Notification for SIGUSR1 (for configuration dump)
   205	        signal.Notify(signalChan, syscall.SIGUSR1)
   206	
   207	        intfMgr := networkinterface.NewManager()
   208	        arpMgr := arp.NewManager(config)
   209	
   210	        // create the node label manager
   211	        // constructor will decide if it should be a noop or not
   212	        nodeLabelManager := node.NewManager(config, clientset)
   213	
   214	        var bgpServer *bgp.Server
   215	        // If BGP is enabled then we start a server instance that will broadcast VIPs
   216	        if config.EnableBGP {
   217	                var err error
   218	                // If Annotations have been set then we will look them up
   219	                if config.Annotations != "" {
   220	                        err = annotationsWatcher(ctx, clientset, rwClientSet, config)
   221	                } else {
   222	                        log.Debug("No Node annotations to parse")
   223	                }
   224	
   225	                if err != nil {
   226	                        return nil, err
   227	                }
   228	
   229	                bgpServer, err = bgp.NewBGPServer(config.BGPConfig)
   230	                if err != nil {
   231	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("creating BGP server: %w", err)
   232	                }
   233	        }
   234	
   235	        electionMgr, err := election.NewManager(config, clientset, rwClientSet)
   236	        if err != nil {
   237	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("creating election manager: %w", err)
   238	        }
   239	
   240	        leaseMgr := lease.NewManager()
   241	
   242	        svcProcessor := services.NewServicesProcessor(config, bgpServer, clientset, rwClientSet,
   243	                intfMgr, arpMgr, nodeLabelManager, electionMgr, leaseMgr)
   244	
   245	        return &Manager{
   246	                clientSet:   clientset,
   247	                rwClientSet: rwClientSet,
   248	                configMap:   configMap,
   249	                config:      config,
   250	                countServiceWatchEvent: prometheus.NewCounterVec(prometheus.CounterOpts{
   251	                        Namespace: "kube_vip",
   252	                        Subsystem: "manager",
   253	                        Name:      "all_services_events",
   254	                        Help:      "Count all events fired by the service watcher categorised by event type",
   255	                }, []string{"type"}),
   256	                bgpSessionInfoGauge: prometheus.NewGaugeVec(prometheus.GaugeOpts{
   257	                        Namespace: "kube_vip",
   258	                        Subsystem: "manager",
   259	                        Name:      "bgp_session_info",
   260	                        Help:      "Display state of session by setting metric for label value with current state to 1",
   261	                }, []string{"state", "peer"}),
   262	                signalChan:       signalChan,
   263	                svcProcessor:     svcProcessor,
   264	                intfMgr:          intfMgr,
   265	                arpMgr:           arpMgr,
   266	                bgpServer:        bgpServer,
   267	                nodeLabelManager: nodeLabelManager,
   268	                electionMgr:      electionMgr,
   269	                leaseMgr:         leaseMgr,
   270	        }, nil
   271	}
   272	
   273	// Start will begin the Manager, which will start services and watch the configmap
   274	func (sm *Manager) Start(ctx context.Context) error {
   275	        wg := sync.WaitGroup{}
   276	        defer wg.Wait()
   277	
   278	        // HealthCheck
   279	        if sm.config.HealthCheckPort != 0 {
   280	                if sm.config.HealthCheckPort < 1024 {
   281	                        return fmt.Errorf("healthcheck port is using a port that is less than 1024 [%d]", sm.config.HealthCheckPort)
   282	                }
   283	                http.HandleFunc("/healthz", func(w http.ResponseWriter, _ *http.Request) {
   284	                        fmt.Fprintf(w, "OK")
   285	                })
   286	                wg.Go(func() {
   287	                        server := &http.Server{
   288	                                Addr:              fmt.Sprintf(":%d", sm.config.HealthCheckPort),
   289	                                ReadHeaderTimeout: 3 * time.Second,
   290	                        }
   291	                        err := server.ListenAndServe()
   292	                        if err != nil {
   293	                                log.Error("healthcheck", "unable to start", err)
   294	                        }
   295	                })
   296	        }
   297	
   298	        // on exit, clean up the node labels
   299	        defer func() {
   300	                if err := sm.nodeLabelManager.CleanUpLabels(10 * time.Second); err != nil {
   301	                        log.Error("CleanUpNodeLabels", "unable to cleanup node labels", err)
   302	                }
   303	        }()
   304	
   305	        if sm.config.EnableARP || sm.config.EnableWireguard {
   306	                if sm.config.EnableUPNP {
   307	                        clients := upnp.GetConnectionClients(ctx)
   308	                        if len(clients) == 0 {
   309	                                log.Error("Error Enabling UPNP. No Clients found")
   310	                                // Set the struct to false so nothing should use it in future
   311	                                sm.config.EnableUPNP = false
   312	                        } else {
   313	                                for _, c := range clients {
   314	                                        ip, err := c.GetExternalIPAddress()
   315	                                        if err != nil {
   316	                                                log.Error("unable to find IGD2 Gateway address", "err", err)
   317	                                        }
   318	                                        log.Info("Found UPNP IGD2 Gateway address", "ip", ip)
   319	                                }
   320	                        }
   321	                        // TODO: It would be nice to run the UPNP refresh only on the leader.
   322	                        wg.Go(func() {
   323	                                sm.svcProcessor.RefreshUPNPForwards(ctx)
   324	                        })
   325	                }
   326	        }
   327	
   328	        return sm.startMode(ctx)
   329	}
   330	
   331	// Start will begin the Manager, which will start services and watch the configmap
   332	func (sm *Manager) startMode(ctx context.Context) error {
   333	        var cpCluster *cluster.Cluster
   334	        var err error
   335	
   336	        w := worker.New(sm.arpMgr, sm.intfMgr, sm.config, &sm.closing, sm.Kill,
   337	                sm.svcProcessor, &sm.mutex, sm.clientSet, sm.bgpServer, sm.bgpSessionInfoGauge,
   338	                sm.electionMgr, sm.leaseMgr)
   339	
   340	        // use a Go context so we can tell the leaderelection code when we
   341	        // want to step down
   342	        wg := sync.WaitGroup{}
   343	        modeCtx, cancel := context.WithCancel(ctx)
   344	        defer func() {
   345	                // wait for gorutines then cancel context just in case
   346	                wg.Wait()
   347	                w.Cleanup()
   348	                cancel()
   349	                log.Info("Shutting down Kube-Vip")
   350	        }()
   351	
   352	        log.Info("starting Kube-vip Manager", "mode", w.Name())
   353	        if err := w.Configure(modeCtx, &wg); err != nil {
   354	                return fmt.Errorf("failed to configure %s mode: %w", w.Name(), err)
   355	        }
   356	
   357	        if sm.config.EnableControlPlane {
   358	                err = w.InitControlPlane()
   359	                if err != nil {
   360	                        return err
   361	                }
   362	        }
   363	
   364	        // Shutdown function that will wait on this signal, unless we call it ourselves
   365	        wg.Go(func() {
   366	                sm.waitForShutdown(modeCtx, cancel, cpCluster)
   367	        })
   368	
   369	        if sm.config.EnableControlPlane {
   370	                wg.Go(func() {
   371	                        w.StartControlPlane(modeCtx, sm.electionMgr)
   372	                })
   373	        }
   374	
   375	        if sm.config.EnableServices {
   376	                // This will tidy any dangling kube-vip iptables rules
   377	                if sm.config.EgressClean {
   378	                        err := nftables.ClearTables()
   379	                        if err != nil {
   380	                                log.Warn("[egress]", "mode", "nftables-internal", "clearing error", err)
   381	                        } else {
   382	                                log.Info("[egress]", "mode", "nftables-internal", "tables", "cleared")
   383	                        }
   384	                        // TODO: Deprecate the iptables code v1.2.x
   385	                        err = vip.ClearIPTables(sm.config.EgressWithNftables, sm.config.ServiceNamespace, iptables.ProtocolIPv4)
   386	                        if err != nil {
   387	                                log.Info("[egress]", "legacy-iptables", sm.config.EgressWithNftables, "mode", "IPv4", "error", err)
   388	                        }
   389	                        err = vip.ClearIPTables(sm.config.EgressWithNftables, sm.config.ServiceNamespace, iptables.ProtocolIPv6)
   390	                        if err != nil {
   391	                                log.Info("[egress]", "legacy-iptables", sm.config.EgressWithNftables, "mode", "IPv6", "error", err)
   392	                        }
   393	                }
   394	                w.ConfigureServices()
   395	
   396	                for {
   397	                        select {
   398	                        case <-modeCtx.Done():
   399	                                return nil
   400	                        default:
   401	                                if err = w.StartServices(modeCtx); err != nil {
   402	                                        if errors.Is(err, &utils.PanicError{}) {
   403	                                                sm.Kill()
   404	                                                return fmt.Errorf("failed to reconcile services, non-recoverable error: %w", err)
   405	                                        } else {
   406	                                                log.Error("failed to reconcile services, restarting", "error", err)
   407	                                        }
   408	                                }
   409	                        }
   410	                }
   411	        }
   412	
   413	        return nil
   414	}
   415	
   416	func (sm *Manager) waitForShutdown(ctx context.Context, cancel context.CancelFunc, cpCluster *cluster.Cluster) {
   417	        for {
   418	                sig := <-sm.signalChan
   419	                switch sig {
   420	                case syscall.SIGUSR1:
   421	                        log.Info("Received SIGUSR1, dumping configuration")
   422	                        sm.dumpConfiguration(ctx)
   423	                case syscall.SIGINT, syscall.SIGTERM:
   424	                        sm.closing.Store(true)
   425	                        log.Info("Received kube-vip termination, signaling shutdown")
   426	                        if cpCluster != nil {
   427	                                cpCluster.Stop()
   428	                        }
   429	                        // Cancel the context, which will in turn cancel the leadership and all goroutines
   430	                        cancel()
   431	                        return
   432	                }
   433	        }
   434	}
   435	
   436	func (sm *Manager) Kill() {
   437	        sm.sigint.Do(func() {
   438	                sm.signalChan <- syscall.SIGINT
   439	        })
   440	}
   441

2026-05-30 01:01:53,038 - INFO - swea-agent-kube-vip__kube-vip-1505 - 💭 THOUGHT


Now I have a clear picture. The issue is in `/testbed/pkg/manager/manager.go` at line 105:

```go
config.NodeName = hostname
```

The `hostname` returned by `os.Hostname()` can contain uppercase characters. According to RFC 1123, node names must be lowercase. Kubernetes node names are always lowercase, and if we use a node name with uppercase characters, service node label updates will fail because the node won't be found in k8s with that name.

The fix is to lowercase the hostname before assigning it to `config.NodeName`.

Let me also check if there are any other places where the hostname might be used as node name and needs lowercasing:



🎬 ACTION

   712	        }

   717	// LoadConfigFromFile loads configuration from a JSON or YAML file
   718	func LoadConfigFromFile(configFilePath string) (*Config, error) {
   719	        if configFilePath == "" {
   720	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("config file path is empty")
   721	        }
   722	
   723	        // Check if file exists
   724	        if _, err := os.Stat(configFilePath); os.IsNotExist(err) {
   725	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("config file does not exist: %s", configFilePath)
   726	        }
   727	
   728	        // Read file content
   729	        data, err := os.ReadFile(configFilePath)
   730	        if err != nil {
   731	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to read config file %s: %v", configFilePath, err)
   732	        }
   733	
   734	        var config Config
   735	        ext := strings.ToLower(filepath.Ext(configFilePath))
   736	
   737	        switch ext {
   738	        case ".json":
   739	                err = json.Unmarshal(data, &config)
   740	                if err != nil {
   741	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to parse JSON config file %s: %v", configFilePath, err)
   742	                }
   743	        case ".yaml", ".yml":
   744	                err = yaml.Unmarshal(data, &config)
   745	                if err != nil {
   746	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to parse YAML config file %s: %v", configFilePath, err)
   747	                }
   748	        default:
   749	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("unsupported config file format %s. Supported formats: .json, .yaml, .yml", ext)
   750	        }
   751	
   752	        return &config, nil
   753	}
   754	
   755	// MergeConfigFromFile merges configuration loaded from file with existing config
   756	// Priority: command line flags > environment variables > config file
   757	func MergeConfigFromFile(c *Config, configFilePath string) error {
   758	        if configFilePath == "" {
   759	                return nil // No config file specified, nothing to merge
   760	        }
   761	
   762	        fileConfig, err := LoadConfigFromFile(configFilePath)
   763	        if err != nil {
   764	                return err
   765	        }
   766	
   767	        // Merge file config with existing config
   768	        // Only set values from file if they haven't been set by flags or env vars
   769	        mergeConfigValues(c, fileConfig)
   770	
   771	        return nil
   772	}
   773

    37	// NewManager creates a new Label Manager for the given node
    38	func NewManager(nodeName string, clientSet *kubernetes.Clientset) *Manager {
    39	        return &Manager{
    40	                nodeName:  nodeName,

    42	        }

    46	type Manager struct {
    47	        // nodeName is the name of the node to manage
    48	        nodeName string
    49	
    50	        // clientSet is the Kubernetes client set to use
    51	        clientSet *kubernetes.Clientset
    52	}

    54	// AddLabel a new label to the node
    55	func (m *Manager) AddLabel(ctx context.Context, svc *corev1.Service) error {
    56	        log.Debug("[service] add label to node", "namespace", svc.Namespace, "name", svc.Name)
    57	        labelKey, labelValue := generateNodeLabelKeyValue(svc)
    58	        return m.patchNode(ctx, labelOperationAdd, map[string]string{labelKey: labelValue})
    59	}
    60	
    61	// RemoveLabel a label from the node
    62	func (m *Manager) RemoveLabel(ctx context.Context, svc *corev1.Service) error {
    63	        log.Debug("[service] delete label from node", "namespace", svc.Namespace, "name", svc.Name)
    64	        labelKey, _ := generateNodeLabelKeyValue(svc)
    65	        return m.patchNode(ctx, labelOperationRemove, map[string]string{labelKey: ""})
    66	}
    67	
    68	// clean up the node labels
    69	func (m *Manager) CleanUpLabels(timeout time.Duration) error {
    70	        log.Debug("cleaning up labels for node", "node", m.nodeName, "timeout", timeout)
    71	
    72	        // create new context for labels cleanup (independent)
    73	        ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), timeout)
    74	        defer cancel()
    75	
    76	        // get the node
    77	        node, err := m.clientSet.CoreV1().Nodes().Get(ctx, m.nodeName, metav1.GetOptions{})
    78	        if err != nil {
    79	                return errors.Wrapf(err, "failed to get node %s", m.nodeName)
    80	        }
    81	
    82	        // collect all labels with the prefix to remove
    83	        labels := map[string]string{}
    84	        for k := range node.Labels {
    85	                if strings.HasPrefix(k, labelName) {
    86	                        labels[k] = ""
    87	                }
    88	        }
    89	
    90	        if len(labels) == 0 {
    91	                log.Debug("no labels to remove for node", "node", m.nodeName)
    92	                return nil
    93	        }
    94	
    95	        // patch the node with the labels to remove
    96	        return m.patchNode(ctx, labelOperationRemove, labels)
    97	}
    98	
    99	// generateNodeLabelKeyValue generates a label key and value for the given service
   100	func generateNodeLabelKeyValue(svc *corev1.Service) (string, string) {
   101	        addresses, _ := instance.FetchServiceAddresses(svc)
   102	
   103	        sanitized := make([]string, len(addresses))
   104	        for i, addr := range addresses {
   105	                sanitized[i] = sanitizeIPForLabel(addr)
   106	        }
   107	
   108	        return fmt.Sprintf("%s/%s.%s", labelName, svc.Name, svc.Namespace), strings.Join(sanitized, ",")
   109	}
   110	
   111	// Helper function to convert IPv6 hex address without colons
   112	func sanitizeIPForLabel(addr string) string {
   113	        ip := net.ParseIP(addr)
   114	        if ip == nil || ip.To4() != nil {
   115	                return addr
   116	        }
   117	        return hex.EncodeToString(ip.To16())
   118	}
   119	
   120	// patchNode patches the node with the given labels
   121	func (m *Manager) patchNode(ctx context.Context, operation labelOperation, labels map[string]string) error {
   122	        type patchStringLabel struct {
   123	                Op    string `json:"op"`
   124	                Path  string `json:"path"`
   125	                Value string `json:"value"`
   126	        }
   127	
   128	        patchLabels := []patchStringLabel{}
   129	        // generate the patch
   130	        for k, v := range labels {
   131	                patchLabels = append(patchLabels, patchStringLabel{
   132	                        Op: string(operation),
   133	                        // replace all slashes with ~1
   134	                        Path:  fmt.Sprintf("/metadata/labels/%s", strings.ReplaceAll(k, "/", "~1")),
   135	                        Value: v,
   136	                })
   137	        }
   138	
   139	        patchData, err := json.Marshal(patchLabels)
   140	        if err != nil {
   141	                log.Debug("node patch marshaling failed", "err", err, "labels", labels, "patch", patchLabels)
   142	                return errors.Wrapf(err, "node patch marshaling failed for labels %v", labels)
   143	        }
   144	
   145	        log.Debug("patching node",
   146	                "node", m.nodeName,
   147	                "patch", string(patchData),
   148	                "operation", operation,
   149	                "labels", labels,
   150	                "clientSetNil", m.clientSet == nil)
   151	        if m.clientSet == nil {
   152	                return errors.New("kubernetes client is not initialized")
   153	        }
   154	
   155	        // patch node
   156	        node, err := m.clientSet.CoreV1().Nodes().Patch(ctx, m.nodeName, types.JSONPatchType, patchData, metav1.PatchOptions{})
   157	        if err != nil {
   158	                log.Debug("node patching failed", "err", err, "patchData", patchData)
   159	                return errors.Wrapf(err, "node patching failed with patch %s", string(patchData))
   160	        }
   161	
   162	        log.Debug("updated", "node", m.nodeName, "labels", node.Labels)
   163	
   164	        return nil
   165	}
   166

    27	// This file handles the watching of node annotations for configuration, it will exit once the annotations are
    28	// present
    29	func annotationsWatcher(ctx context.Context, clientSet,
    30	        rwClientSet kubernetes.Interface, config *kubevip.Config) error {
    31	        // Use a restartable watcher, as this should help in the event of etcd or timeout issues
    32	        log.Info("Kube-Vip is waiting for annotation prefix to be present on this node", "prefix", config.Annotations)
    33	
    34	        labelSelector := metav1.LabelSelector{MatchLabels: map[string]string{"kubernetes.io/hostname": config.NodeName}}
    35	        listOptions := metav1.ListOptions{
    36	                LabelSelector: labels.Set(labelSelector.MatchLabels).String(),
    37	        }
    38	
    39	        // First we'll check the annotations for the node and if
    40	        // they aren't what are expected, we'll drop into the watch until they are
    41	        nodeList, err := clientSet.CoreV1().Nodes().List(ctx, listOptions)
    42	        if err != nil {
    43	                return err
    44	        }
    45	
    46	        // We'll assume there's only one node with the hostname annotation. If that's not true,
    47	        // there's probably bigger problems
    48	        node := nodeList.Items[0]
    49	
    50	        bgpConfig, bgpPeer, err := parseBgpAnnotations(config.BGPConfig, &node, config.Annotations)
    51	        if err == nil {
    52	                // No error, the annotations already exist
    53	                config.BGPConfig = bgpConfig
    54	                config.BGPPeerConfig = bgpPeer
    55	                return nil
    56	        }
    57	
    58	        // We got an error with the annotations, falling back to the watch until
    59	        // they're as needed
    60	        log.Warn(err.Error())
    61	
    62	        rw, err := watchtools.NewRetryWatcherWithContext(ctx, node.ResourceVersion, &cache.ListWatch{
    63	                WatchFunc: func(_ metav1.ListOptions) (watch.Interface, error) {
    64	                        return rwClientSet.CoreV1().Nodes().Watch(ctx, listOptions)
    65	                },
    66	        })
    67	
    68	        if err != nil {
    69	                return fmt.Errorf("error creating annotations watcher: %s", err.Error())
    70	        }
    71	
    72	        defer func() {
    73	                rw.Stop()
    74	                log.Debug("[annotations] watcher stopped")
    75	        }()
    76	
    77	        ch := rw.ResultChan()
    78	
    79	        for event := range ch {
    80	                // We need to inspect the event and get ResourceVersion out of it
    81	                switch event.Type {
    82	                case watch.Added, watch.Modified:
    83	                        node, ok := event.Object.(*v1.Node)
    84	                        if !ok {
    85	                                return fmt.Errorf("unable to parse Kubernetes Node from Annotation watcher")
    86	                        }
    87	
    88	                        bgpConfig, bgpPeer, err := parseBgpAnnotations(config.BGPConfig, node, config.Annotations)
    89	                        if err != nil {
    90	                                log.Error(err.Error())
    91	                                continue
    92	                        }
    93	
    94	                        config.BGPConfig = bgpConfig
    95	                        config.BGPPeerConfig = bgpPeer
    96	
    97	                        log.Info("[annotations] exiting Annotations watcher - annotations found")
    98	                        return nil
    99	                case watch.Deleted:
   100	                        node, ok := event.Object.(*v1.Node)
   101	                        if !ok {
   102	                                return fmt.Errorf("unable to parse Kubernetes Node from Kubernetes watcher")
   103	                        }
   104	
   105	                        log.Info("Node has been deleted", "name", node.Name)
   106	
   107	                case watch.Bookmark:
   108	                        // Un-used
   109	                case watch.Error:
   110	                        log.Error("Error attempting to watch Kubernetes Nodes")
   111	
   112	                        // This round trip allows us to handle unstructured status
   113	                        errObject := apierrors.FromObject(event.Object)
   114	                        statusErr, ok := errObject.(*apierrors.StatusError)
   115	                        if !ok {
   116	                                log.Error(spew.Sprintf("Received an error which is not *metav1.Status but %#+v", event.Object))
   117	
   118	                        }
   119	
   120	                        status := statusErr.ErrStatus
   121	                        log.Error(status.String())
   122	                default:
   123	                }
   124	        }
   125	        log.Info("[annotations] exiting annotations watcher")
   126	        return nil
   127	}
   128	
   129	// parseNodeAnnotations parses the annotations on the node and updates the configuration
   130	// returning an error if the annotations are not valid or missing; and nil if everything is OK
   131	// to continue
   132	//
   133	// Parsed annotation config overlays config in passed bgpConfig in order to preserve configs
   134	// set by other means with the exception that bgpConfig.Peers is overwritten.
   135	//
   136	// The regex expression for each annotation ensures (at least in terms of annotations) backwards
   137	// compatibility with the Equinix Metal annotation format changed in
   138	// https://github.com/equinix/cloud-provider-equinix-metal/releases/tag/v3.3.0
   139	//
   140	// "metal.equinix.com/<info>`" --> "metal.equinix.com/bgp-peers-{{n}}-<info>`"
   141	// * `<info>` is the relevant information, such as `node-asn` or `peer-ip`
   142	// * `{{n}}` is the number of the peer, always starting with `0`
   143	// * kube-vip is only designed to manage one peer, just look for {{n}} == 0
   144	func parseBgpAnnotations(bgpConfig kubevip.BGPConfig, node *v1.Node, prefix string) (kubevip.BGPConfig, kubevip.BGPPeer, error) {
   145	        bgpPeer := kubevip.BGPPeer{}
   146	
   147	        prefix = regexp.QuoteMeta(prefix)
   148	
   149	        nodeASN := ""
   150	        regex := regexp.MustCompile(fmt.Sprintf("^%s/(bgp-peers-0-)?node-asn$", prefix))
   151	        for k, v := range node.Annotations {
   152	                if regex.Match([]byte(k)) {
   153	                        nodeASN = v
   154	                }
   155	        }
   156	        if nodeASN == "" {
   157	                return bgpConfig, bgpPeer, fmt.Errorf("node-asn value missing or empty")
   158	        }
   159	
   160	        u64, err := strconv.ParseUint(nodeASN, 10, 32)
   161	        if err != nil {
   162	                return bgpConfig, bgpPeer, err
   163	        }
   164	
   165	        bgpConfig.AS = uint32(u64)
   166	
   167	        srcIP := ""
   168	        regex = regexp.MustCompile(fmt.Sprintf("^%s/(bgp-peers-0-)?src-ip$", prefix))
   169	        for k, v := range node.Annotations {
   170	                if regex.Match([]byte(k)) {
   171	                        srcIP = v
   172	                }
   173	        }
   174	        if srcIP == "" {
   175	                return bgpConfig, bgpPeer, fmt.Errorf("src-ip value missing or empty")
   176	        }
   177	
   178	        // Set the routerID (Unique ID for BGP) to the source IP
   179	        // Also set the BGP peering to the sourceIP
   180	        bgpConfig.RouterID, bgpConfig.SourceIP = srcIP, srcIP
   181	
   182	        peerASN := ""
   183	        regex = regexp.MustCompile(fmt.Sprintf("^%s/(bgp-peers-0-)?peer-asn$", prefix))
   184	        for k, v := range node.Annotations {
   185	                if regex.Match([]byte(k)) {
   186	                        peerASN = v
   187	                }
   188	        }
   189	        if peerASN == "" {
   190	                return bgpConfig, bgpPeer, fmt.Errorf("peer-asn value missing or empty")
   191	        }
   192	
   193	        u64, err = strconv.ParseUint(peerASN, 10, 32)
   194	        if err != nil {
   195	                return bgpConfig, bgpPeer, err
   196	        }
   197	
   198	        bgpPeer.AS = uint32(u64)
   199	
   200	        peerIPString := ""
   201	        regex = regexp.MustCompile(fmt.Sprintf("^%s/(bgp-peers-[0-9]+-)?peer-ip$", prefix))
   202	        for k, v := range node.Annotations {
   203	                if regex.Match([]byte(k)) {
   204	                        peerIPString += v + ","
   205	                }
   206	        }
   207	        peerIPString = strings.TrimRight(peerIPString, ",")
   208	
   209	        peerIPs := strings.Split(peerIPString, ",")
   210	        if len(peerIPs) >= 1 && peerIPs[0] == "" || len(peerIPs) == 0 {
   211	                return bgpConfig, bgpPeer, fmt.Errorf("peer-ip value missing or empty")
   212	        }
   213	
   214	        bgpConfig.Peers = make([]kubevip.BGPPeer, 0, len(peerIPs))
   215	        regexPass := regexp.MustCompile(fmt.Sprintf("^%s/(bgp-peers-0-)?bgp-pass$", prefix))
   216	        regexMultiHop := regexp.MustCompile(fmt.Sprintf("^%s/(bgp-peers-0-)?peer-multi-hop$", prefix))
   217	        for _, peerIP := range peerIPs {
   218	                ipAddr := strings.TrimSpace(peerIP)
   219	
   220	                if ipAddr != "" {
   221	                        bgpPeer.Address = ipAddr
   222	                        // Check if we're also expecting a password for this peer
   223	                        base64BGPPassword := ""
   224	                        for k, v := range node.Annotations {
   225	                                if regexPass.Match([]byte(k)) {
   226	                                        base64BGPPassword = v
   227	                                }
   228	                        }
   229	                        if base64BGPPassword != "" {
   230	                                // Decode base64 encoded string
   231	                                decodedPassword, err := base64.StdEncoding.DecodeString(base64BGPPassword)
   232	                                if err != nil {
   233	                                        return bgpConfig, bgpPeer, err
   234	                                }
   235	                                // Set the password for each peer
   236	                                bgpPeer.Password = string(decodedPassword)
   237	                        }
   238	
   239	                        // Check if multi-hop is enabled.
   240	                        for k, v := range node.Annotations {
   241	                                if regexMultiHop.MatchString(k) {
   242	                                        switch v {
   243	                                        case "true":
   244	                                                bgpPeer.MultiHop = true
   245	                                        case "false":
   246	                                                bgpPeer.MultiHop = false
   247	                                        default:
   248	                                                return bgpConfig, bgpPeer,
   249	                                                        fmt.Errorf("invalid %q annotation value: %q, must be \"true\" or \"false\"", k, v)
   250	                                        }
   251	                                }
   252	                        }
   253	                        bgpConfig.Peers = append(bgpConfig.Peers, bgpPeer)
   254	                }
   255	        }
   256	
   257	        //log.Debugf("BGPConfig: %v\n", bgpConfig)
   258	        //log.Debugf("BGPPeerConfig: %v\n", bgpPeer)
   259	
   260	        return bgpConfig, bgpPeer, nil
   261	}
   262

    40	// Manager degines the manager of the load-balancing services
    41	type Manager struct {

    52

    54	        signalChan chan os.Signal
    55	
    56	        sigint sync.Once
    57	
    58	        svcProcessor *services.Processor
    59	
    60	        // This is a prometheus counter used to count the number of events received

    62	        countServiceWatchEvent *prometheus.CounterVec
    63

    67

    70

    72	        intfMgr *networkinterface.Manager
    73	
    74	        // This tracks VIPs and performs ARP/NDP advertisement.
    75	        arpMgr *arp.Manager
    76

    78	        // implementation will be decided in constructor

    81

    90	}
    91	
    92	// New will create a new managing object
    93	func New(ctx context.Context, configMap string, config *kubevip.Config) (*Manager, error) {
    94	
    95	        // Instance identity should be the same as k8s node name to ensure better compatibility.
    96	        // By default k8s sets node name to `hostname -s`,
    97	        // so if node name is not provided in the config,
    98	        // we set it to hostname as a fallback.
    99	        // This mimics legacy behavior and should work on old kube-vip installations.
   100	        if config.NodeName == "" {
   101	                log.Warn("Node name is missing from the config, fall back to hostname")
   102	                hostname, err := os.Hostname()
   103	                if err != nil {
   104	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not get hostname: %v", err)
   105	                }
   106	                config.NodeName = strings.ToLower(hostname)
   107	        }
   108	        log.Info("using node name", "name", config.NodeName)
   109	
   110	        adminConfigPath := "/etc/kubernetes/admin.conf"

package main

import (
    "fmt"
    "os"
    "strings"
)

func main() {
    // Simulate the OLD behavior
    hostname, err := os.Hostname()
    if err != nil {
        fmt.Printf("Error getting hostname: %v\n", err)
        return
    }
    
    // If we had an uppercase hostname, the old code would have kept it uppercase
    oldBehavior := hostname
    // New behavior lowercases it
    newBehavior := strings.ToLower(hostname)
    
    fmt.Printf("Hostname from OS: [%s]\n", hostname)
    fmt.Printf("Old behavior (NodeName): [%s]\n", oldBehavior)
    fmt.Printf("New behavior (NodeName): [%s]\n", newBehavior)
    fmt.Printf("RFC 1123 compliant: %v\n", newBehavior == strings.ToLower(newBehavior))
    
    // Simulate an uppercase hostname
    testUppercase := "MY-HOST.EXAMPLE.COM"
    fmt.Printf("\nSimulated uppercase hostname: [%s]\n", testUppercase)
    fmt.Printf("After strings.ToLower: [%s]\n", strings.ToLower(testUppercase))
}
EOF
go run /tmp/verify_fix.go

All tests pass. Now let me also consider edge cases:

1. **Empty hostname after lowercasing**: `strings.ToLower("")` returns `""`, which is fine - the hostname from `os.Hostname()` should never be empty if there's no error.

2. **Already lowercase hostname**: `strings.ToLower` on an already lowercase string is a no-op, so it's safe.

3. **Mixed case hostname**: E.g., `My-Host.Example.Com` → `my-host.example.com` - correct.

4. **All uppercase hostname**: E.g., `MYHOST` → `myhost` - correct.

5. **Hostname with special characters**: `strings.ToLower` only affects ASCII letters, so special characters like hyphens, dots, etc. remain unchanged, which is correct for RFC 1123.

Let me also check if there are any other places in the codebase where the node name might be used without lowercasing. Looking at the config_environment.go line 108-110:

```go
env = os.Getenv(nodeName)
if env != "" {
    c.NodeName = env
}
```

This is when the user explicitly sets the node name via environment variable. In this case, we should probably also lowercase it, because the user might set an uppercase node name by mistake. But the PR description says "Node names should be rfc1123 compliant even when falling back on os.Hostname()", so the fix should be focused on the fallback path.

However, let me think about this more carefully. The PR says:

> "It is possible to have hostnames for machines contain uppercase characters; even if you keep the hostname for the node name it will be lower cased for rfc1123."

So the issue is specifically about the fallback to `os.Hostname()`. The environment variable `vip_nodename` is explicitly set by the user, so it's the user's responsibility to provide a correct value there. But to be thorough, let me also check if there's anything in the config file path that might need lowercasing.

Looking at `config_environment.go` line 801-802:
```go
if baseConfig.NodeName == "" && fileConfig.NodeName != "" {
    baseConfig.NodeName = fileConfig.NodeName
}
```

This merges from file config. Again, this is user-provided, so it's the user's responsibility.

The key fix is the `os.Hostname()` fallback, which I've already addressed.

 // New will create a new managing object
 func New(ctx context.Context, configMap string, config *kubevip.Config) (*Manager, error) {
 
-	// Instance identity should be the same as k8s node name to ensure better compatibility.
-	// By default k8s sets node name to `hostname -s`,
-	// so if node name is not provided in the config,

+        // Instance identity should be the same as k8s node name to ensure better compatibility.
+        // By default k8s sets node name to `hostname -s`,
+        // so if node name is not provided in the config,
+        // we set it to hostname as a fallback.
+        // This mimics legacy behavior and should work on old kube-vip installations.
+        if config.NodeName == "" {
+                log.Warn("Node name is missing from the config, fall back to hostname")
+                hostname, err := os.Hostname()
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not get hostname: %v", err)
+                }
+                config.NodeName = strings.ToLower(hostname)
+        }
+        log.Info("using node name", "name", config.NodeName)
+
+        adminConfigPath := "/etc/kubernetes/admin.conf"
+        homeConfigPath := filepath.Join(os.Getenv("HOME"), ".kube", "config")
+
+        var clientset *kubernetes.Clientset
+        var clientConfig *rest.Config
+        var err error
+
+        switch {
+        case config.LeaderElectionType == "etcd":
+                // Do nothing, we don't construct a k8s client for etcd leader election
+        case utils.FileExists(adminConfigPath):
+                if config.KubernetesAddr != "" {
+                        log.Info("k8s address", "address", config.KubernetesAddr)
+                        clientConfig, err = k8s.NewRestConfig(adminConfigPath, false, config.KubernetesAddr)
+                } else if config.EnableControlPlane {
+                        // If this is a control plane host it will likely have started as a static pod or won't have the
+                        // VIP up before trying to connect to the API server, we set the API endpoint to this machine to
+                        // ensure connectivity.
+                        if config.DetectControlPlane {
+                                clientConfig, err = k8s.FindWorkingKubernetesAddress(adminConfigPath, false)
+                        } else {
+                                // This will attempt to use kubernetes as the hostname (this should be passed as a host alias) in the pod manifest
+                                clientConfig, err = k8s.NewRestConfig(adminConfigPath, false, fmt.Sprintf("kubernetes:%v", config.Port))
+                        }
+                } else {
+                        clientConfig, err = k8s.NewRestConfig(adminConfigPath, false, "")
+                }
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s REST config from external file: %q: %w", adminConfigPath, err)
+                }
+                if clientset, err = k8s.NewClientset(clientConfig); err != nil {
+                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s clientset: %w", err)
+                }
+                log.Debug("Using external Kubernetes configuration from file", "path", adminConfigPath)
+        case utils.FileExists(homeConfigPath):
+                clientConfig, err = k8s.NewRestConfig(homeConfigPath, false, "")
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s REST config from external file: %q: %w", homeConfigPath, err)
+                }
+                clientset, err = k8s.NewClientset(clientConfig)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s clientset from external file: %q: %w", homeConfigPath, err)
+                }
+                log.Debug("Using external Kubernetes configuration from file", "path", adminConfigPath)
+        default:
+                clientConfig, err = k8s.NewRestConfig("", true, "")
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s REST config from incluster file: %q: %w", homeConfigPath, err)
+                }
+                clientset, err = k8s.NewClientset(clientConfig)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s clientset from incluster config: %w", err)
+                }
+                log.Debug("Using external Kubernetes configuration from incluster config.")
+        }
+
+        var rwClientSet *kubernetes.Clientset
+        // if clientConfig is not nil, then we are not using etcd leader election
+        // we need to create non-timeout clientset for RetryWatcher
+        if clientConfig != nil {
+                rwConfig := *clientConfig
+                rwConfig.Timeout = 0
+                rwClientSet, err = k8s.NewClientset(&rwConfig)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s clientset for retry watcher: %w", err)
+                }
+        }
+
+        // Flip this to something else
+        // if config.DetectControlPlane {
+        //      log.Info("[k8s client] flipping to internal service account")
+        //      _, err = clientset.CoreV1().ServiceAccounts("kube-system").Apply(context.TODO(), kubevip.GenerateSA(), v1.ApplyOptions{FieldManager: "application/apply-patch"})
+        //      if err != nil {
+        //              return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s clientset from incluster config: %v", err)
+        //      }
+        //      _, err = clientset.RbacV1().ClusterRoles().Apply(context.TODO(), kubevip.GenerateCR(), v1.ApplyOptions{FieldManager: "application/apply-patch"})
+        //      if err != nil {
+        //              return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s clientset from incluster config: %v", err)
+        //      }
+        //      _, err = clientset.RbacV1().ClusterRoleBindings().Apply(context.TODO(), kubevip.GenerateCRB(), v1.ApplyOptions{FieldManager: "application/apply-patch"})
+        //      if err != nil {
+        //              return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s clientset from incluster config: %v", err)
+        //      }
+        // }
+
+        // listen for interrupts or the Linux SIGTERM signal and cancel
+        // our context, which the leader election code will observe and
+        // step down
+        signalChan := make(chan os.Signal, 1)
+        // Add Notification for Userland interrupt
+        signal.Notify(signalChan, syscall.SIGINT)
+
+        // Add Notification for SIGTERM (sent from Kubernetes)
+        signal.Notify(signalChan, syscall.SIGTERM)
+
+        // Add Notification for SIGUSR1 (for configuration dump)
+        signal.Notify(signalChan, syscall.SIGUSR1)
+
+        intfMgr := networkinterface.NewManager()
+        arpMgr := arp.NewManager(config)
+
+        // create the node label manager
+        // constructor will decide if it should be a noop or not
+        nodeLabelManager := node.NewManager(config, clientset)
+
+        var bgpServer *bgp.Server
+        // If BGP is enabled then we start a server instance that will broadcast VIPs
+        if config.EnableBGP {
+                var err error
+                // If Annotations have been set then we will look them up
+                if config.Annotations != "" {
+                        err = annotationsWatcher(ctx, clientset, rwClientSet, config)
+                } else {
+                        log.Debug("No Node annotations to parse")
+                }
+
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, err
+                }
+
+                bgpServer, err = bgp.NewBGPServer(config.BGPConfig)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("creating BGP server: %w", err)
+                }
+        }
+
+        electionMgr, err := election.NewManager(config, clientset, rwClientSet)
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, fmt.Errorf("creating election manager: %w", err)
+        }
+
+        leaseMgr := lease.NewManager()
+
+        svcProcessor := services.NewServicesProcessor(config, bgpServer, clientset, rwClientSet,
+                intfMgr, arpMgr, nodeLabelManager, electionMgr, leaseMgr)
+
+        return &Manager{
+                clientSet:   clientset,
+                rwClientSet: rwClientSet,
+                configMap:   configMap,
+                config:      config,
+                countServiceWatchEvent: prometheus.NewCounterVec(prometheus.CounterOpts{
+                        Namespace: "kube_vip",
+                        Subsystem: "manager",
+                        Name:      "all_services_events",
+                        Help:      "Count all events fired by the service watcher categorised by event type",
+                }, []string{"type"}),
+                bgpSessionInfoGauge: prometheus.NewGaugeVec(prometheus.GaugeOpts{
+                        Namespace: "kube_vip",
+                        Subsystem: "manager",
+                        Name:      "bgp_session_info",
+                        Help:      "Display state of session by setting metric for label value with current state to 1",
+                }, []string{"state", "peer"}),
+                signalChan:       signalChan,
+                svcProcessor:     svcProcessor,
+                intfMgr:          intfMgr,
+                arpMgr:           arpMgr,
+                bgpServer:        bgpServer,
+                nodeLabelManager: nodeLabelManager,
+                electionMgr:      electionMgr,
+                leaseMgr:         leaseMgr,
+        }, nil
 }

+                        }
+                })
+        }
+
+        // on exit, clean up the node labels

+                        log.Error("CleanUpNodeLabels", "unable to cleanup node labels", err)

+                                sm.config.EnableUPNP = false
+                        } else {
+                                for _, c := range clients {
+                                        ip, err := c.GetExternalIPAddress()
+                                        if err != nil {
+                                                log.Error("unable to find IGD2 Gateway address", "err", err)
+                                        }
+                                        log.Info("Found UPNP IGD2 Gateway address", "ip", ip)
+                                }
+                        }
+                        // TODO: It would be nice to run the UPNP refresh only on the leader.
+                        wg.Go(func() {
+                                sm.svcProcessor.RefreshUPNPForwards(ctx)
+                        })
+                }
+        }

+        // Shutdown function that will wait on this signal, unless we call it ourselves
+        wg.Go(func() {
+                sm.waitForShutdown(modeCtx, cancel, cpCluster)
+        })
+
+        if sm.config.EnableControlPlane {
+                wg.Go(func() {
+                        w.StartControlPlane(modeCtx, sm.electionMgr)
+                })
+        }
+
+        if sm.config.EnableServices {
+                // This will tidy any dangling kube-vip iptables rules
+                if sm.config.EgressClean {
+                        err := nftables.ClearTables()
+                        if err != nil {
+                                log.Warn("[egress]", "mode", "nftables-internal", "clearing error", err)
+                        } else {
+                                log.Info("[egress]", "mode", "nftables-internal", "tables", "cleared")
+                        }
+                        // TODO: Deprecate the iptables code v1.2.x
+                        err = vip.ClearIPTables(sm.config.EgressWithNftables, sm.config.ServiceNamespace, iptables.ProtocolIPv4)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                log.Info("[egress]", "legacy-iptables", sm.config.EgressWithNftables, "mode", "IPv4", "error", err)
+                        }
+                        err = vip.ClearIPTables(sm.config.EgressWithNftables, sm.config.ServiceNamespace, iptables.ProtocolIPv6)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                log.Info("[egress]", "legacy-iptables", sm.config.EgressWithNftables, "mode", "IPv6", "error", err)
+                        }
+                }
+                w.ConfigureServices()
+
+                for {
+                        select {
+                        case <-modeCtx.Done():
+                                return nil
+                        default:
+                                if err = w.StartServices(modeCtx); err != nil {
+                                        if errors.Is(err, &utils.PanicError{}) {
+                                                sm.Kill()
+                                                return fmt.Errorf("failed to reconcile services, non-recoverable error: %w", err)
+                                        } else {
+                                                log.Error("failed to reconcile services, restarting", "error", err)
+                                        }
+                                }
+                        }
+                }
+        }
+
+        return nil
 }
 
 func (sm *Manager) waitForShutdown(ctx context.Context, cancel context.CancelFunc, cpCluster *cluster.Cluster) {
-	for {
-		sig := <-sm.signalChan
-		switch sig {
-		case syscall.SIGUSR1:
-			log.Info("Received SIGUSR1, dumping configuration")
-			sm.dumpConfiguration(ctx)
-		case syscall.SIGINT, syscall.SIGTERM:
-			sm.closing.Store(true)
-			log.Info("Received kube-vip termination, signaling shutdown")
-			if cpCluster != nil {
-				cpCluster.Stop()
-			}
-			// Cancel the context, which will in turn cancel the leadership and all goroutines
-			cancel()
-			return
-		}
-	}
+        for {
+                sig := <-sm.signalChan
+                switch sig {
+                case syscall.SIGUSR1:
+                        log.Info("Received SIGUSR1, dumping configuration")
+                        sm.dumpConfiguration(ctx)
+                case syscall.SIGINT, syscall.SIGTERM:
+                        sm.closing.Store(true)
+                        log.Info("Received kube-vip termination, signaling shutdown")
+                        if cpCluster != nil {
+                                cpCluster.Stop()
+                        }
+                        // Cancel the context, which will in turn cancel the leadership and all goroutines
+                        cancel()
+                        return
+                }
+        }
 }
 
 func (sm *Manager) Kill() {
-	sm.sigint.Do(func() {
-		sm.signalChan <- syscall.SIGINT
-	})
+        sm.sigint.Do(func() {
+                sm.signalChan <- syscall.SIGINT
+        })
 }

+        // This mimics legacy behavior and should work on old kube-vip installations.
+        if config.NodeName == "" {
+                log.Warn("Node name is missing from the config, fall back to hostname")
+                hostname, err := os.Hostname()
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not get hostname: %v", err)
+                }
+                config.NodeName = strings.ToLower(hostname)
+        }
+        log.Info("using node name", "name", config.NodeName)
+
+        adminConfigPath := "/etc/kubernetes/admin.conf"
+        homeConfigPath := filepath.Join(os.Getenv("HOME"), ".kube", "config")
+
+        var clientset *kubernetes.Clientset
+        var clientConfig *rest.Config
+        var err error
+
+        switch {
+        case config.LeaderElectionType == "etcd":
+                // Do nothing, we don't construct a k8s client for etcd leader election
+        case utils.FileExists(adminConfigPath):
+                if config.KubernetesAddr != "" {
+                        log.Info("k8s address", "address", config.KubernetesAddr)
+                        clientConfig, err = k8s.NewRestConfig(adminConfigPath, false, config.KubernetesAddr)
+                } else if config.EnableControlPlane {
+                        // If this is a control plane host it will likely have started as a static pod or won't have the
+                        // VIP up before trying to connect to the API server, we set the API endpoint to this machine to
+                        // ensure connectivity.
+                        if config.DetectControlPlane {
+                                clientConfig, err = k8s.FindWorkingKubernetesAddress(adminConfigPath, false)
+                        } else {
+                                // This will attempt to use kubernetes as the hostname (this should be passed as a host alias) in the pod manifest
+                                clientConfig, err = k8s.NewRestConfig(adminConfigPath, false, fmt.Sprintf("kubernetes:%v", config.Port))
+                        }
+                } else {
+                        clientConfig, err = k8s.NewRestConfig(adminConfigPath, false, "")
+                }
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s REST config from external file: %q: %w", adminConfigPath, err)
+                }
+                if clientset, err = k8s.NewClientset(clientConfig); err != nil {
+                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s clientset: %w", err)
+                }
+                log.Debug("Using external Kubernetes configuration from file", "path", adminConfigPath)
+        case utils.FileExists(homeConfigPath):
+                clientConfig, err = k8s.NewRestConfig(homeConfigPath, false, "")
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s REST config from external file: %q: %w", homeConfigPath, err)
+                }
+                clientset, err = k8s.NewClientset(clientConfig)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s clientset from external file: %q: %w", homeConfigPath, err)
+                }
+                log.Debug("Using external Kubernetes configuration from file", "path", adminConfigPath)
+        default:
+                clientConfig, err = k8s.NewRestConfig("", true, "")
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s REST config from incluster file: %q: %w", homeConfigPath, err)
+                }
+                clientset, err = k8s.NewClientset(clientConfig)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s clientset from incluster config: %w", err)
+                }
+                log.Debug("Using external Kubernetes configuration from incluster config.")
+        }
+
+        var rwClientSet *kubernetes.Clientset
+        // if clientConfig is not nil, then we are not using etcd leader election
+        // we need to create non-timeout clientset for RetryWatcher
+        if clientConfig != nil {
+                rwConfig := *clientConfig
+                rwConfig.Timeout = 0
+                rwClientSet, err = k8s.NewClientset(&rwConfig)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s clientset for retry watcher: %w", err)
+                }
+        }
+
+        // Flip this to something else
+        // if config.DetectControlPlane {
+        //      log.Info("[k8s client] flipping to internal service account")
+        //      _, err = clientset.CoreV1().ServiceAccounts("kube-system").Apply(context.TODO(), kubevip.GenerateSA(), v1.ApplyOptions{FieldManager: "application/apply-patch"})
+        //      if err != nil {

+        //      }

+        //      if err != nil {
+        //              return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not create k8s clientset from incluster config: %v", err)
+        //      }
+        //      _, err = clientset.RbacV1().ClusterRoleBindings().Apply(context.TODO(), kubevip.GenerateCRB(), v1.ApplyOptions{FieldManager: "application/apply-patch"})
+        //      if err != nil {

+        // listen for interrupts or the Linux SIGTERM signal and cancel
+        // our context, which the leader election code will observe and
+        // step down
+        signalChan := make(chan os.Signal, 1)
+        // Add Notification for Userland interrupt
+        signal.Notify(signalChan, syscall.SIGINT)
+
+        // Add Notification for SIGTERM (sent from Kubernetes)
+        signal.Notify(signalChan, syscall.SIGTERM)
+
+        // Add Notification for SIGUSR1 (for configuration dump)
+        signal.Notify(signalChan, syscall.SIGUSR1)
+
+        intfMgr := networkinterface.NewManager()
+        arpMgr := arp.NewManager(config)
+
+        // create the node label manager
+        // constructor will decide if it should be a noop or not
+        nodeLabelManager := node.NewManager(config, clientset)
+
+        var bgpServer *bgp.Server
+        // If BGP is enabled then we start a server instance that will broadcast VIPs
+        if config.EnableBGP {
+                var err error
+                // If Annotations have been set then we will look them up
+                if config.Annotations != "" {
+                        err = annotationsWatcher(ctx, clientset, rwClientSet, config)
+                } else {
+                        log.Debug("No Node annotations to parse")
+                }
+
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, err
+                }
+
+                bgpServer, err = bgp.NewBGPServer(config.BGPConfig)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("creating BGP server: %w", err)
+                }
+        }
+
+        electionMgr, err := election.NewManager(config, clientset, rwClientSet)
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, fmt.Errorf("creating election manager: %w", err)
+        }
+
+        leaseMgr := lease.NewManager()
+
+        svcProcessor := services.NewServicesProcessor(config, bgpServer, clientset, rwClientSet,
+                intfMgr, arpMgr, nodeLabelManager, electionMgr, leaseMgr)
+
+        return &Manager{
+                clientSet:   clientset,
+                rwClientSet: rwClientSet,
+                configMap:   configMap,
+                config:      config,
+                countServiceWatchEvent: prometheus.NewCounterVec(prometheus.CounterOpts{
+                        Namespace: "kube_vip",
+                        Subsystem: "manager",
+                        Name:      "all_services_events",
+                        Help:      "Count all events fired by the service watcher categorised by event type",
+                }, []string{"type"}),
+                bgpSessionInfoGauge: prometheus.NewGaugeVec(prometheus.GaugeOpts{
+                        Namespace: "kube_vip",
+                        Subsystem: "manager",
+                        Name:      "bgp_session_info",
+                        Help:      "Display state of session by setting metric for label value with current state to 1",
+                }, []string{"state", "peer"}),
+                signalChan:       signalChan,
+                svcProcessor:     svcProcessor,
+                intfMgr:          intfMgr,
+                arpMgr:           arpMgr,
+                bgpServer:        bgpServer,
+                nodeLabelManager: nodeLabelManager,
+                electionMgr:      electionMgr,
+                leaseMgr:         leaseMgr,
+        }, nil
 }

-					log.Info("Found UPNP IGD2 Gateway address", "ip", ip)
-				}
-			}

+        wg := sync.WaitGroup{}
+        defer wg.Wait()
+
+        // HealthCheck
+        if sm.config.HealthCheckPort != 0 {
+                if sm.config.HealthCheckPort < 1024 {
+                        return fmt.Errorf("healthcheck port is using a port that is less than 1024 [%d]", sm.config.HealthCheckPort)
+                }
+                http.HandleFunc("/healthz", func(w http.ResponseWriter, _ *http.Request) {
+                        fmt.Fprintf(w, "OK")
+                })
+                wg.Go(func() {
+                        server := &http.Server{
+                                Addr:              fmt.Sprintf(":%d", sm.config.HealthCheckPort),
+                                ReadHeaderTimeout: 3 * time.Second,
+                        }
+                        err := server.ListenAndServe()
+                        if err != nil {
+                                log.Error("healthcheck", "unable to start", err)
+                        }
+                })
+        }
+
+        // on exit, clean up the node labels
+        defer func() {
+                if err := sm.nodeLabelManager.CleanUpLabels(10 * time.Second); err != nil {
+                        log.Error("CleanUpNodeLabels", "unable to cleanup node labels", err)
+                }
+        }()
+
+        if sm.config.EnableARP || sm.config.EnableWireguard {
+                if sm.config.EnableUPNP {
+                        clients := upnp.GetConnectionClients(ctx)
+                        if len(clients) == 0 {
+                                log.Error("Error Enabling UPNP. No Clients found")
+                                // Set the struct to false so nothing should use it in future
+                                sm.config.EnableUPNP = false
+                        } else {
+                                for _, c := range clients {
+                                        ip, err := c.GetExternalIPAddress()
+                                        if err != nil {
+                                                log.Error("unable to find IGD2 Gateway address", "err", err)
+                                        }
+                                        log.Info("Found UPNP IGD2 Gateway address", "ip", ip)
+                                }
+                        }
+                        // TODO: It would be nice to run the UPNP refresh only on the leader.
+                        wg.Go(func() {
+                                sm.svcProcessor.RefreshUPNPForwards(ctx)
+                        })
+                }
+        }
+
+        return sm.startMode(ctx)
 }

+        var cpCluster *cluster.Cluster
+        var err error
+
+        w := worker.New(sm.arpMgr, sm.intfMgr, sm.config, &sm.closing, sm.Kill,
+                sm.svcProcessor, &sm.mutex, sm.clientSet, sm.bgpServer, sm.bgpSessionInfoGauge,
+                sm.electionMgr, sm.leaseMgr)
+
+        // use a Go context so we can tell the leaderelection code when we
+        // want to step down
+        wg := sync.WaitGroup{}
+        modeCtx, cancel := context.WithCancel(ctx)
+        defer func() {
+                // wait for gorutines then cancel context just in case
+                wg.Wait()
+                w.Cleanup()
+                cancel()
+                log.Info("Shutting down Kube-Vip")
+        }()
+
+        log.Info("starting Kube-vip Manager", "mode", w.Name())
+        if err := w.Configure(modeCtx, &wg); err != nil {
+                return fmt.Errorf("failed to configure %s mode: %w", w.Name(), err)
+        }
+
+        if sm.config.EnableControlPlane {
+                err = w.InitControlPlane()
+                if err != nil {
+                        return err
+                }
+        }
+
+        // Shutdown function that will wait on this signal, unless we call it ourselves
+        wg.Go(func() {
+                sm.waitForShutdown(modeCtx, cancel, cpCluster)
+        })
+
+        if sm.config.EnableControlPlane {
+                wg.Go(func() {
+                        w.StartControlPlane(modeCtx, sm.electionMgr)
+                })
+        }
+
+        if sm.config.EnableServices {
+                // This will tidy any dangling kube-vip iptables rules
+                if sm.config.EgressClean {
+                        err := nftables.ClearTables()
+                        if err != nil {
+                                log.Warn("[egress]", "mode", "nftables-internal", "clearing error", err)
+                        } else {
+                                log.Info("[egress]", "mode", "nftables-internal", "tables", "cleared")
+                        }
+                        // TODO: Deprecate the iptables code v1.2.x
+                        err = vip.ClearIPTables(sm.config.EgressWithNftables, sm.config.ServiceNamespace, iptables.ProtocolIPv4)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                log.Info("[egress]", "legacy-iptables", sm.config.EgressWithNftables, "mode", "IPv4", "error", err)
+                        }
+                        err = vip.ClearIPTables(sm.config.EgressWithNftables, sm.config.ServiceNamespace, iptables.ProtocolIPv6)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                log.Info("[egress]", "legacy-iptables", sm.config.EgressWithNftables, "mode", "IPv6", "error", err)
+                        }
+                }
+                w.ConfigureServices()
+
+                for {
+                        select {
+                        case <-modeCtx.Done():
+                                return nil
+                        default:
+                                if err = w.StartServices(modeCtx); err != nil {
+                                        if errors.Is(err, &utils.PanicError{}) {
+                                                sm.Kill()
+                                                return fmt.Errorf("failed to reconcile services, non-recoverable error: %w", err)
+                                        } else {
+                                                log.Error("failed to reconcile services, restarting", "error", err)
+                                        }
+                                }
+                        }
+                }
+        }
+
+        return nil
 }

-		sig := <-sm.signalChan

-				cpCluster.Stop()
-			}
-			// Cancel the context, which will in turn cancel the leadership and all goroutines

-		}
-	}
+        for {
+                sig := <-sm.signalChan
+                switch sig {
+                case syscall.SIGUSR1:
+                        log.Info("Received SIGUSR1, dumping configuration")
+                        sm.dumpConfiguration(ctx)
+                case syscall.SIGINT, syscall.SIGTERM:
+                        sm.closing.Store(true)
+                        log.Info("Received kube-vip termination, signaling shutdown")
+                        if cpCluster != nil {
+                                cpCluster.Stop()
+                        }
+                        // Cancel the context, which will in turn cancel the leadership and all goroutines
+                        cancel()
+                        return
+                }
+        }
 }

+        })
 }
